## ğŸ’¡ How to Run

### Installation

#### Clone The Repository
```bash
$ git clone https://github.com/2023-Summer-Bootcamp-Team-K/docker.git
```

#### Emulator ì‹¤í–‰
```bash
$ cd docker/frontend
$ flutter pub get
$ flutter doctor
$ flutter run
```

#### Backend í™˜ê²½ë³€ìˆ˜ ì„¤ì •

backend/.env
```bash
DB_NAME =
DB_USER =
DB_PASSWORD = 
DB_HOST = 

AMAZON_ACCESS_KEY = 
AMAZON_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY =

SECRET_KEY = 

LIBRE_ID = 
LIBRE_PASSWORD =

GOOGLE_ID = 
GOOGLE_PASSWORD = 
```

#### ê°œë°œ ì„œë²„
```bash
$ docker-compose up --d
```
